msg:I stayed at the Yunji No.1 Cliff Seaview Hotel in Haidong Town, Dali, for one night with my parents. The hotel has stunning Santorini-style architecture, and we could see the beautiful Erhai Lake from our room. The hotel is very artistic, and most of the decorations are related to the theme of jade or emerald. The most impressive thing for me was the largest natural night pearl in the world, which was displayed in the hotel‚Äôs restaurant. It was so amazing to see it glowing in the dark.

The hotel‚Äôs butler Whisky(Miss Wei) was a lovely, gentle, and beautiful lady. She contacted me before our arrival, hand-wrote and drew our welcome cards and illustrations. She also arranged extra beds and breakfasts for us, considering that we were traveling with our parents. I think she was very attentive and helpful throughout our stay, and she made our experience so wonderful.

The hotel is also close to some attractions, such as the Three Pagodas and the Butterfly Spring. We enjoyed exploring the local culture and nature.

We had a great time at the  Yunji, and we would definitely recommend it to anyone who wants to visit Dali. It was one of the best hotels we have ever stayed at.
